</header><div class="entry-content"><div class="tasty-pins-hidden-image-container" style="display:none;"><img alt="Cutting board of ingredients and pan and plate of Simple Vegetable Tempeh Stir Fry" class="tasty-pins-hidden-image" data-pin-description="DELICIOUS and EASY Vegetable Tempeh Stir Fry! 30 minutes, 10 ingredients, BIG flavor, SO satisfying! #vegan #glutenfree #dinner #tempeh #stirfry #minimalistbaker #recipe" data-pin-media="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry.jpg" data-pin-title="30-Minute Tempeh Stir-Fry" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry-200x200.jpg"/></div>
<input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"/><p><img alt="Overhead image of tempeh quinoa stir fry in a cast iron pot with a small serving plate and chopsticks on the side" class="aligncenter wp-image-39121 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="30-Minute Tempeh Stir-Fry" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/" data-jpibfi-src="http://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/DELICIOUS-and-EASY-Vegetable-Tempeh-Stir-Fry-30-minutes-10-ingredients-BIG-flavor-SO-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-dinner-tempeh-stirfry-minimalistbaker-recipe-6.jpg" data-pin-description="DELICIOUS and EASY Vegetable Tempeh Stir Fry! <p>Everyone needs a good, classic stir fry recipe in their back pocket for quick lunches and dinners, and I think this should be the one.</p>
<p>It comes together in just <strong>30 minutes</strong>, uses up leftover grains and vegetables from the week, is rich in protein and fiber, and delivers big flavor. What’s not to love? Let me show you how easy it is to get this dish on the table.</p>
<p><img alt="Overhead image of cutting board with ingredients for a tempeh stir fry including tempeh quinoa bell pepper green onion and kale" class="aligncenter wp-image-39124 size-full" 680w" width="1456"/><span id="more-39131"></span></p>
<p>It all starts with marinating the tempeh. Cube your tempeh, mix with your peanut-coconut aminos (or tamari) glaze, and set aside. While that’s happening you’ll prep your other ingredients.</p>
<p><img alt="Overhead image of bowl with tempeh marinating in peanut sauce and a spoon for stirring" class="aligncenter wp-image-39118 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="30-Minute Tempeh Stir-Fry" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/" data-jpibfi-src="http://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/DELICIOUS-and-EASY-Vegetable-Tempeh-Stir-Fry-30-minutes-10-ingredients-BIG-flavor-SO-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-dinner-tempeh-stirfry-minimalistbaker-recipe-3.jpg" data-pin-description="DELICIOUS and EASY Vegetable Tempeh Stir Fry! 30 minutes, 10 ingredients, BIG flavor, SO satisfying! #vegan #glutenfree #dinner #tempeh #stirfry #minimalistbaker #recipe" data-pin-id="" data-pin-media="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry.jpg" data-pin-title="" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/DELICIOUS-and-EASY-Vegetable-Tempeh-Stir-Fry-30-minutes-10-ingredients-BIG-flavor-SO-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-dinner-tempeh-stirfry-minimalistbaker-recipe-3.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/DELICIOUS-and-EASY-Vegetable-Tempeh-Stir-Fry-30-minutes-10-ingredients-BIG-flavor-SO-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-dinner-tempeh-stirfry-minimalistbaker-recipe-3.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/DELICIOUS-and-EASY-Vegetable-Tempeh-Stir-Fry-30-minutes-10-ingredients-BIG-flavor-SO-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-dinner-tempeh-stirfry-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/DELICIOUS-and-EASY-Vegetable-Tempeh-Stir-Fry-30-minutes-10-ingredients-BIG-flavor-SO-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-dinner-tempeh-stirfry-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/DELICIOUS-and-EASY-Vegetable-Tempeh-Stir-Fry-30-minutes-10-ingredients-BIG-flavor-SO-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-dinner-tempeh-stirfry-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/DELICIOUS-and-EASY-Vegetable-Tempeh-Stir-Fry-30-minutes-10-ingredients-BIG-flavor-SO-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-dinner-tempeh-stirfry-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/DELICIOUS-and-EASY-Vegetable-Tempeh-Stir-Fry-30-minutes-10-ingredients-BIG-flavor-SO-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-dinner-tempeh-stirfry-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p><iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/31DPKHwRc0c" width="680"></iframe></p>
<p>Once marinated, sauté your tempeh on both sides until golden brown and delicious. Then you’ll add your veggies and grains and stir-fry until crispy and browned before adding your tempeh back to the pan to warm. That’s it!</p>

<p>We hope you LOVE this stir fry! It’s:</p>
<p>Quick &amp; easy to make<br/>
Incredibly flavorful<br/>
Vegetable-packed<br/>
Protein- &amp; fiber-rich<br/>
&amp; So delicious</p>
<p>This would make the perfect weeknight meal when you want something hearty and nutritious on the table fast. I also love making it for lunch when I want something fast and filling.</p>
<p>If you’re into stir fries, be sure to check out our <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/30-minute-cauliflower-rice-stir-fry/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Cauliflower Rice Stir-Fry</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/30-minute-quinoa-fried-rice/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Quinoa “Fried Rice,”</a> <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/almond-butter-tofu-stir-fry/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Almond Butter Tofu Stir-Fry</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/tofu-that-tastes-good-stir-fry/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Tofu that Tastes Good Stir-Fry</a>, and the fan favorite <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/general-tsos-tofu/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">General Tso’s Tofu Stir-Fry</a>!</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name">30-Minute Tempeh Stir-Fry</h2>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary">
<p>A hearty tempeh stir fry with BIG flavor! Just 30 minutes to prepare this weeknight dinner to use up leftover vegetables and please a crowd!</p> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-author-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-author-name">Author:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author">Minimalist Baker</span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-times-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-name">Prep Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time wprm-recipe-prep_time-minutes">20</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time-unit wprm-recipe-prep_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-name">Cook Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time wprm-recipe-cook_time-minutes">10</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time-unit wprm-recipe-cook_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-total-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-total-time-name">Total Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time wprm-recipe-total_time-minutes">30</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time-unit wprm-recipe-total_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
</div>

<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Ingredients</h3>
<div class="wprm-unit-conversion-container"><a class="wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active" data-recipe="39340" data-system="1" href="#">US Customary</a> - <a class="wprm-unit-conversion" data-recipe="39340" data-system="2" href="#">Metric</a></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">GLAZE</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3-4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://www.amazon.com/dp/B000LO25RG/ref=as_at?creativeASIN=B000LO25RG&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=.6csbbG-X9jkJMCNN2BEcA&amp;slotNum=28&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">chili garlic sauce </a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(adjust to preferred spice level)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">salted creamy peanut butter </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or almond, cashew, or sunflower butter)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sesame oil </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(if avoiding oil, sub water)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Coconut-Secret-Raw-Aminos-Pack/dp/B00CMYMRL2/?tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">coconut aminos </a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub slightly lesser amount of tamari to taste as it can be more pungent in flavor)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">lime juice</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">freshly grated ginger </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub 1/2 tsp ground ginger)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">maple syrup </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(plus more to taste)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3-4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">water</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">TEMPEH</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">8</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">ounces</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">tempeh</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(chopped into large, bite-size squares // if GF, ensure gluten-free friendly)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">THE REST</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sesame oil </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub double this amount in water)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2/3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">chopped green onion</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cups</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">mixed chopped vegetables </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(we used red bell pepper, broccoli, carrots &amp; kale)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Coconut-Secret-Raw-Aminos-Pack/dp/B00CMYMRL2/?tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">coconut aminos </a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or tamari)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cups</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">leftover cooked quinoa,* brown rice,* or uncooked cauliflower rice*</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Instructions</h3>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Prepare glaze by adding chili garlic sauce, peanut butter, sesame oil, coconut aminos (or tamari), lime juice, fresh ginger, and maple syrup to a small mixing bowl. Whisk to combine.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Add water until a thin, pourable sauce is formed. Taste and adjust flavor as needed, adding more chili garlic sauce for heat, maple syrup for sweetness, lime juice for acidity, or coconut aminos for saltiness. Don't be shy — you want this quite flavorful.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Add the chopped tempeh to the glaze and toss to coat. Then cover and refrigerate for 15 minutes (or cover and refrigerate up to 24-48 hours). Prep your other vegetables and toppings at this time.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Heat a large rimmed cast iron or metal skillet over medium heat. Once hot, spoon in the tempeh, reserving most of the glaze in the bowl (set aside for later). Sauté for 3-4 minutes, turning on each side until browned. Then remove from pan and set aside.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>To the still-hot skillet add sesame oil, green onion, and mixed vegetables (if adding greens, wait to add until step 6). Season with a bit of coconut aminos (or tamari) and stir to coat. Cover to cook and steam the vegetables, stirring occasionally until slightly golden brown and tender (about 4-5 minutes). If they stick to the pan, add 1-2 tsp of water to loosen.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Once the vegetables are nearly done, add your greens and grains and sauté for 3-4 minutes or until warmed through and slightly browned. Then add in the cooked tempeh and the rest of the glaze and stir to coat. Cook for another 1-2 minutes, or until everything is hot and well incorporated.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Store leftovers covered in the refrigerator up to 4-5 days. If freezing, store in the freezer up to 1 month. Let thaw before reheating in a hot skillet with a little sesame oil.</div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Made this tonight! So good! My daughter was surprised , impressed and very thankful! She loved it!  Loved how the tempeh browns up.  Think next time will cut it even smaller or even crumble to get more goodness covering more of it.  I used what I had, mushrooms, red pepper, broccoli , carrots and green onion.  Broccoli really gets the flavor in it  thank you so so much for this amazing simple recipe!  (We also did not add the quinoa but served the stir fry on top of it.  )</p>

Also on another note I used tahini in place of a nut butter and sriracha instead of chili garlic sauce as thats what I had and it was still insanely good. Even my toddler who likes zero spice ate some. Thx for another yummy vegan recipe!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>I originally had pulled up a different recipe, but I had a few spare minutes for meal prep and decided to make the sauce. I realized after I made it that it was a different recipe – your recipe. What a happy, happy mistake. I used  to struggle with the chewy texture of tempeh until I started to steam it for 15 minutes. After steaming I let it marinate for the day.  So versatile, I used zucchini, mushrooms, red pepper and the green onion. We will be making this again for sure. Thank you!</p>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-852630">
<article id="article-comment-852630">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Susan" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/184b53a31927bfe20ef6d2464052b970?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/184b53a31927bfe20ef6d2464052b970?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Susan" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Susan</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-852630">December 29, 2019 at 5:26 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was my first attempt at tempeh. I loved the taste, but I scorched the exterior pretty badly. I was sceptical about sauteeing the tempeh with the sauce and no oil…I had a well seasoned cast iron skillet but it immediately stuck although I heated pan first. I removed it to a non-stick skillet, but after one minute on low it burned some more. I still ate it but the carnivores opted for air fried chicken nuggets (ugh). They loved the sauce and veggies….I  used the same ones you used. I will try again, but I’ve never had luck with tofu marinated and sauteed…the sauce was pretty thick on it though I’d thinned it out. I guess I just need to keep experimenting because the flavors are excellent.</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-851578">December 22, 2019 at 8:04 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Excellent recipe! I’m only about 2 months into my Vegan journey and I’m sure I’ll make this recipe many more times. As with every recipe I learn something new, this attempt was no different. Initially my iron skillet was way too hot and I burnt some of the tempeh but no worries I simply scraped it off and proceeded.<br/>
Bc I used only 2 cups brown rice I added Shirataki noodles, added a nice twist. Looking forward to using this great glaze with other dishes, thank u!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Wow! I’ve been looking for a great tempeh recipe. This was so good. I only had soy sauce so used that instead of aminos and siracha instead of chili garlic sauce. I used almond butter and whatever veggies I had around.   I mixed it with leftover quinoa and I am so happy. I am super satisfied and my house smells incredible. I don’t write reviews very often. This one was worth taking the time to say thanks!</p>

<li class="comment even thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-821025">
<article id="article-comment-821025">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Sally" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fa599e663677513cde546f5c8e2ac955?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fa599e663677513cde546f5c8e2ac955?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Sally" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Sally</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-821025">August 18, 2019 at 6:45 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I was looking for something new and different to do with tempeh and came across this recipe. I substituted almost everything to use what I had on hand, and this still came out tasty! The tempeh fried up deliciously crunchy. I used Newman’s Own peach salsa with 2 cloves of chopped garlic added, sunflower butter, olive oil, tamari with a touch of smoke flavoring, lemon juice, ground ginger, maple syrup, a light touch of ground chipotle pepper for the glaze in about the proportions indicated. I fried the tempeh until it looked like your photo, stir fried my veggies, added the rest of the glaze and cooked a bit more then added the tempeh back in. Served on brown basmati rice. Everyone liked it. I’ll definitely make it again.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>I just made this and have some not so positive feedback. Some modifications: I substituted siracha &amp; garlic for the chili-garlic sauce and a tad less peanut butter than called for because that was all I had. I don’t think these changes made a difference, since the flavor was pretty good.  So here goes. I wouldn’t consider this a quick weeknight meal unless you are using pre-cut veggies. It took me an hour to make this and I am an experienced cook. Second, it is tough to fit 4 cups of veggies + greens and 3 cups of grains into a large cast iron pan and still be able to stir. I had to transfer to my oversized sauce pan. Not a big deal. Finally and probably most importantly, the addition of quinoa made this go completely south for me.  It basically turned to veggies mashed together with quinoa. The tempeh was lost. The dish didn’t even need the quinoa.  Without it there would have been enough sauce but it turned into a big mushy mess.  Sorry!</p>
<div class="wprm-comment-rating">
<span class="wprm-rating-stars"><span class="wprm-rating-star"><svg height="16px" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="16px" x="0px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" <div class="comment-content">
<p>It was an MB week at my house!  I made your portobello mushroom pizzas, eggplant parm, and rounded out the week with this tempeh stir fry.  Wow, this stir fry was delicious!  I absolutely loved the tempeh glaze and let it marinate the tempeh overnight.  The veggies I used was broccoli, bell pepper, carrots, green onion, and a zucchini from our home garden.  This dish is so versatile, and I love the idea of using it when you need to “clean out the fridge” and you can customize it with lots of different veggies.  10/10 will make again!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>This has been in super heavy rotation since the day I first tried this! I have been waiting for this recipe all my life I think. I have used basmati rice and quinoa – I like the rice better even though I love quinoa.  I usually just crumble half a block of tofu in instead of marinated tempeh. So easy.  I keep the chili sauce out of the sauce so it’s not too spicy for my 3 year old, and my husband and I just  drizzle it on top after serving. Sometimes we add toasted cashews if we’re feeling extra.</p>

<article id="article-comment-807475">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Sean Okonsky" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/e54fcae8e4202bba3f0510864f176d7d?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/e54fcae8e4202bba3f0510864f176d7d?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Sean Okonsky" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Sean Okonsky</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-807475">June 4, 2019 at 8:03 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I think I already gave a review of this recipe but I had to give another because its that’s good. Since I first made this recipe about 3 months ago I’ve been making it at least once a week. Its quick, easy, tasty, and filling. It works for either lunch or dinner. I grill the red bell pepper, red onion, and Anaheim pepper after the tempeh has cooked for a bit and then add in shredded carrot, cooked quinoa, green onion , and the leftover marinade after I turn the heat off. I top with kimchi, vegan mayo, sesame seeds and cilantro.</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-800972">
<article id="article-comment-800972">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Mother of Corgis" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/4574f80056ed98f7f0dbe37ca37dbb5f?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/4574f80056ed98f7f0dbe37ca37dbb5f?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Mother of Corgis" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Mother of Corgis</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-800972">May 2, 2019 at 6:25 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I was looking for a tempeh recipe with lots of veggies and gave this a shot. Pleasantly surprised, although I felt it was missing a few elements, hence 4 stars.</p>
<p>I used 2 tsp of the chili garlic sauce (because you can always add more), soy sauce instead of tamari, and a bag of frozen stir fry veggies instead of fresh. I also used 1/2 almond butter and 1/2 peanut butter. Next time I’ll use 100% crunchy peanut butter for a richer flavor and texture, which this recipe needs. It’s pretty much ALL softer foods, and although I liked it, it was a bit…homogenous. There was no crunch aside from the water chestnuts in the stir-fry mix. And yes I realize that starting with frozen veggies was going to add more moisture, so next time I’ll leave the lid off so there’s more sauteing (for crispier veggies) and less steaming (for softer veggies). I might even try baking the tempeh so it’s a little more interesting to chew. I’ll probably crush some peanuts and toast them to sprinkle as a garnish, too. And maybe add some fresh cilantro, because c’mon, it’s stir fry.</p>
<p>I’d also urge cooks to use sesame oil, not olive or canola. There is a nutty flavor to sesame oil that’s just perfect in the sauce. I’m sure peanut oil would also be delicious. My husband really, really enjoyed this dish and I know I can elevate it to something I’ll enjoy just as much as he does. It’s a very well-written &amp; versatile recipe, and I’m already looking forward to experimenting with it again.</p>
<div class="wprm-comment-rating">

<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was incredible! Be warned if you, like me, have a fairly low tolerance for spicy food – I only used 2 tsp of chili garlic sauce, and that was just about as spicy as I could have possibly handled, but it was still DELICIOUS! I also used closer to 2 cups of quinoa instead of 3 because the proportions looked about right at 2, which could have been a factor in the spiciness level. Overall though, what a flavorful, healthy, and filling meal!</p>

<p>I found this recipe a couple weeks ago and it is my new favorite. Its healthy, quick, tastes great and works well for either lunch or dinner. I love adding Kim chi and cashew mayo to mine. Thanks for the recipe!</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-784954">February 6, 2019 at 3:25 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made this as directed,  (used almond buttter and rice)and it tasted good. But.,,,strongly recommend that the tempeh is cut into small cubes – no more than an inch square.  Due to the marinade, it blackens easily, so lower heat a bit. I have had more sucess browning the tempeh first, and then marinating.  My vegan family was not impressed.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Dana,<br/>
I have always been suspicious of tempeh, so bland, so naaaahhh, but this recipe of yours just NAILED IT! Oh I can’t stop eating, it’s so delicious. The layering of flavours is just perfect. I used more vegetables: bok chow, red pepper, broccoli, green onions and kale. I overcooked the kale (darn) so I won’t be posting a picture anywhere because the colours are a bit off, but the flavour is to die for. My stovetop is now a mess but it’s so worth it!!! You’re the very best, Dana.</p>

<p>My husband and I both loved this. We marinated the tempeh for the minimum time, used a little extra chili garlic sauce, and choose red bell pepper, shredded carrots, broccoli, spinach, and shiitake mushrooms for our vegetables. We probably had 5-6 cups of vegetables rather than the 4 and it worked well other than my 10-inch see was almost overflowing. This is going to be a go-to easy, healthy meal for us.</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-782369">January 18, 2019 at 4:57 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was AMAZING.  I used tamari and it somehow was too salty but tasted amazing on the quinoa/brown rice mixture I made.  The veggies I used were rainbow carrots, chopped kale, mushrooms, zucchini (I forgot onion).  I’m adding this to my weekly recipes.  I’ve only ever had tempeh this good one other time.  It charred quickly in the stainless steel pan I had on medium high heat w cooking spray and was phenomenal.  Great recipe!!</p>

<article id="article-comment-782208">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Claire" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/e7ecec90c462ae37d3b751f1dc5053cb?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/e7ecec90c462ae37d3b751f1dc5053cb?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Claire" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Claire</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-782208">January 17, 2019 at 4:42 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was yummy! A bit longer than 30 minutes (closer to 60), but that’s mainly because I’m quite a slow cook. Since I’m not vegan or gf, I used soy sauce and honey in place of coconut aminos and maple syrup. I also subbed 2 garlic cloves and a teaspoon of red pepper flakes for the chili garlic sauce. Super delicious!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>My two year old and I are chowing down on this right now and enjoying it immensely! Since hubbie isn’t a fan of soy I subbed with “chicken” seitan and then used onions and broccoli for the veggies. It goes beautifully with quinoa and has a nice spice to it (so I’m especially pleased that the baby likes it). Definitely a repeat dish!</p>

<img alt="Avatar for Casey Mullen" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/7e7daa90ee7451b006422fa700ceb602?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/7e7daa90ee7451b006422fa700ceb602?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Casey Mullen" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Casey Mullen</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-781949">January 15, 2019 at 12:44 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Hi Claudia :) you don’t necessarily have to boil or steam tempeh before use. Some people recommend this because it can help counteract some of the natural bitterness that tempeh has. You can definitely do this if you would like, but I’m guessing with the bold flavors of the glaze in this recipe it’s probably not necessary.</p>
</div>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-781929">January 15, 2019 at 9:38 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Subs for chili garlic sauce, anyone? Subs for maple syrup?  Thanks :)</p>
</div>
<div class="comment-reply"><a aria-label="Reply to Rupini" class="comment-reply-link" data-belowelement="comment-781929" data-commentid="781929" data-postid="39131" data-respondelement="respond" href="#comment-781929" rel="nofollow">Reply</a></div>
</article>
<ul class="children">
<li class="comment even depth-2" id="comment-781951">
<article id="article-comment-781951">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Casey Mullen" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/7e7daa90ee7451b006422fa700ceb602?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/7e7daa90ee7451b006422fa700ceb602?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Casey Mullen" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Casey Mullen</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-781951">January 15, 2019 at 12:52 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>For chili garlic sauce, you could use sriracha. Or even just some chili flakes and minced garlic. Chili garlic sauce is basically just a mix of vinegar, chili flakes, garlic paste, and sometimes a little sugar. You can easily DIY it if you want :) for maple syrup you could substitute any liquid sweetener, like honey, brown rice syrup, coconut nectar, agave nectar, etc. If you can’t get ahold of any of those, you could probably just use a little bit of brown sugar.</p>
</div>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/simple-vegetable-tempeh-stir-fry/?t=1582413800#comment-782111">January 17, 2019 at 6:38 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>You don’t need to boil tempeh! It just needs to be cooked, which you do when sautéing. If you want though, you can steam it for 10 minutes, which supposedly helps remove some of the bitterness. But, it’s totally optional.</p>
</div>
